class=3D"entry-content clearfix"> <h2>First analysis</h2> <p>The first step in this challenge was to analyze the entire package. We w= ere presented with a IOS mobile application.</p> <pre><code><span style=3D"font-size: 14px;">root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <= span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">ls -alh</span> total 72K drwxr-xr-x 4 root root 4.0K May 3 2018 . drwxr-xr-x 4 root root 4.0K Aug 2 13:21 .. drwxr-xr-x 4 root root 4.0K May 3 2018 Base.lproj -rw-r--r-- 1 root root 185 May 3 2018 challenge.plist drwxr-xr-x 2 root root 4.0K May 3 2018 _CodeSignature -rw-r--r-- 1 root root 32K May 3 2018 hackthebox -rw-r--r-- 1 root root 9.6K May 3 2018 htb-company.png -rw-r--r-- 1 root root 1.2K May 3 2018 Info.plist -rw-r--r-- 1 root root 8 May 3 2018 PkgInfo</span></code></pre> <p>Since the plist files were not easily readable, I started to research th= is as the challenge.plist file seemed to contain an interesting base64 stri= ng. After finding <a href=3D"http://osxdaily.com/2016/03/10/convert-plist-f= ile-xml-binary-mac-os-x-plutil/" target=3D"_blank" rel=3D"noopener noreferr= er">this article on converting plist files to XML</a>, I quickly found the = plistutil tool for linux and was able to find the base64 encoded/encrypted = flag</p> <pre><code><span style=3D"font-size: 14px;">root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <= span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">plistutil -i challenge.plist -o challenge.pl= ist.xml</span> root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">cat challenge= .plist.xml</span>=20 <?xml version=3D"1.0" encoding=3D"UTF-8"?> <!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN" "http://www.apple.c= om/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd"> <plist version=3D"1.0"> <array> <dict> <key>flag</key> <string><span style=3D"color: #0000ff;">Tq+CWzQS0wYzs2rJ+GNrPLP6qek= Dbwze6fIeRRwBK2WXHOhba7WR2OGNUFKoAvyW7njTCMlQzlwIRdJvaP2iYQ=3D=3D</span><= ;/string> <key>id</key> <string>123</string> <key>title</key> <string>HackTheBoxIsCool</string> </dict> </array> </plist> </span></code></pre> <h2>Reverse Engineering</h2> <p>According to the Hackthebox Forums, some reverse engineering would be re= quired too. So I decided to give <a href=3D"https://ghidra-sre.org/" target= =3D"_blank" rel=3D"noopener noreferrer">the NSA=E2=80=99s Ghidra</a> a try.= Using Ghidra, I was able to identify some interesting functions and disect= them into the Key and IV value</p> <p><img data-attachment-id=3D"1692" data-permalink=3D"https://www.vanderzie= l.org/2019/08/02/hackthebox-cryptohorrific/crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functio= ns/" data-orig-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderziel.org/wp-content/uplo= ads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functions.png?fit=3D433%2C264&ssl= =3D1" data-orig-size=3D"433,264" data-comments-opened=3D"1" data-image-meta= =3D"{"aperture":"0","credit":"",&qu= ot;camera":"","caption":"","created= _timestamp":"0","copyright":"","foc= al_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_s= peed":"0","title":"","orientation&q= uot;:"0"}" data-image-title=3D"crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functions= " data-image-description=3D"<p>ghidra symboltree containing function names<= /p> " data-image-caption=3D"" data-medium-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderz= iel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functions.png?f= it=3D300%2C183&ssl=3D1" data-large-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vander= ziel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functions.png?= fit=3D433%2C264&ssl=3D1" class=3D"size-full wp-image-1692 alignnone jet= pack-lazy-image jetpack-lazy-image--handled" src=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.v= anderziel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_symboltree_functions= .png?resize=3D433%2C264&ssl=3D1" alt=3D"ghidra symboltree containing fu= nction names" width=3D"433" height=3D"264" data-recalc-dims=3D"1" data-lazy= -loaded=3D"1" loading=3D"eager"></p> <p>By looking at this overview, the SecretManager function appeared interes= ting but further analysis showed that it uses Apple=E2=80=99s CCCrypt, this= function did not (yet) help me much. Looking further to where the function= was called upon, appeared to be in the viewDidLoad function. This function= call showed also the Key and IV value</p> <p><img data-attachment-id=3D"1693" data-permalink=3D"https://www.vanderzie= l.org/2019/08/02/hackthebox-cryptohorrific/crypto_ghidra_interesting_functi= on/" data-orig-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderziel.org/wp-content/uplo= ads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_interesting_function.png?fit=3D682%2C66&ssl= =3D1" data-orig-size=3D"682,66" data-comments-opened=3D"1" data-image-meta= =3D"{"aperture":"0","credit":"",&qu= ot;camera":"","caption":"","created= _timestamp":"0","copyright":"","foc= al_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_s= peed":"0","title":"","orientation&q= uot;:"0"}" data-image-title=3D"crypto_ghidra_interesting_function= " data-image-description=3D"<p>part of the viewDidLoad function, containing= a function call to the SecretManager</p> " data-image-caption=3D"" iel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_interesting_function.png?f= it=3D682%2C66&ssl=3D1" class=3D"size-full wp-image-1693 alignnone jetpa= ck-lazy-image jetpack-lazy-image--handled" src=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.van= derziel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra_interesting_function.p= ng?resize=3D682%2C66&ssl=3D1" alt=3D"part of the viewDidLoad function, = containing a function call to the SecretManager" width=3D"682" height=3D"66= " data-recalc-dims=3D"1" data-lazy-loaded=3D"1" loading=3D"eager"></p> <p>These same entries also appeared a little further down in the Symbol Tre= e were  very likely to be the encryption Key and IV values..</p> <p><img data-attachment-id=3D"1690" data-permalink=3D"https://www.vanderzie= l.org/2019/08/02/hackthebox-cryptohorrific/crypto_ghidra/" data-orig-file= =3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderziel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_= ghidra.png?fit=3D433%2C311&ssl=3D1" data-orig-size=3D"433,311" data-com= ments-opened=3D"1" data-image-meta=3D"{"aperture":"0",&= quot;credit":"","camera":"","captio= n":"","created_timestamp":"0","copy= right":"","focal_length":"0","iso&q= uot;:"0","shutter_speed":"0","title"= ;:"","orientation":"0"}" data-image-title=3D"= crypto_ghidra" data-image-description=3D"<p>Ghidra used to identify interes= ting elements in the hackthebox binary</p> " data-image-caption=3D"" data-medium-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderz= iel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra.png?fit=3D300%2C215&ss= l=3D1" data-large-file=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderziel.org/wp-content/u= ploads/2019/08/crypto_ghidra.png?fit=3D433%2C311&ssl=3D1" class=3D"size= -full wp-image-1690 alignnone jetpack-lazy-image jetpack-lazy-image--handle= d" src=3D"https://i0.wp.com/www.vanderziel.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/c= rypto_ghidra.png?resize=3D433%2C311&ssl=3D1" alt=3D"ghidra used to iden= tify interesting elements" width=3D"433" height=3D"311" data-recalc-dims=3D= "1" data-lazy-loaded=3D"1" loading=3D"eager"></p> <h2>Finding the flag</h2> <p>According to <a href=3D"https://stackoverflow.com/questions/27014292/ccc= rypt-decrypting-in-aes-cbc-works-even-without-iv" target=3D"_blank" rel=3D"= noopener noreferrer">this stackoverflow post</a>, the IV value is not requi= red at all and therefore I continued with just one of the values to be conv= erted into a Hexadecimal key as that is required in the openssl decryption = command.</p> <pre><code><span style=3D"font-size: 14px;">root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <= span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">echo -n '!AD*G-KaPdSgVkY' | xxd -pu</span>= =20 2141442a472d4b6150645367566b59</span></code></pre> <p>Since I was unable to determine which AES cipher was used, I decided to = put them all in one file and loop over all of them with the hex value of th= e key. This provided a number of =E2=80=98hex string to short=E2=80=99 erro= rs, but also provided the HTB Flag.</p> <pre><code><span style=3D"font-size: 14px;">root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <= span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">cat aes</span>=20 ---snip--- aes-256-ctr aes-128-ofb aes-192-ofb aes-256-ofb aes-128-ecb aes-192-ecb aes-256-ecb root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">cat string</s= pan>=20 <span style=3D"color: #0000ff;">Tq+CWzQS0wYzs2rJ+GNrPLP6qekDbwze6fIeRRwBK2W= XHOhba7WR2OGNUFKoAvyW7njTCMlQzlwIRdJvaP2iYQ=3D=3D</span> root@kalivm:~/cryptohorrific# <span style=3D"color: #ff0000;">for i in `cat= aes`; do cat string | openssl enc -d -$i -K 214125442A472D4B6150645367566B= 59 -iv 0 -nopad -nosalt -base64; done</span> hex string is too short, padding with zero bytes to length =EF=BF=BD2/=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BD#V=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BD\V=EF=BF=BD#=EF= =BF=BDg=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BD uS@0=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BDj=EF=BF=BDY#=EF=BF=BDF0 ?=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF=BDg>a=EF=BF=BD7D=EF=BF=BDc=EF=BF=BD=EF=BF= =BDkP=EF=BF=BDvx ---snip--- <span style=3D"color: #ffcc00;"><strong>HTB{%SoC00l_H4ckTh3b<noflag>u= r31stCh4ll3ng3!!Cr4zY%}</strong></span> ---snip---</span></code></pre> <div class=3D"sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled"><div class=3D"robots-nocontent= sd-block sd-social sd-social-official sd-sharing"><h3 class=3D"sd-title">S= hare this:</h3><div class=3D"sd-content"><ul data-sharing-events-added=3D"t= rue"><li class=3D"share-email share-service-visible"><a rel=3D"nofollow noo= pener noreferrer" data-shared=3D"" class=3D"share-email sd-button" href=3D"= mailto:?subject=3D%5BShared%20Post%5D%20Hackthebox%20-%20Cryptohorrific&= ;body=3Dhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.vanderziel.org%2F2019%2F08%2F02%2Fhackthebox-cryp= tohorrific%2F&share=3Demail&nb=3D1" target=3D"_blank" title=3D"Clic= k to email a link to a friend" data-email-share-error-title=3D"Do you have = email set up?" data-email-share-error-text=3D"If you're having problems sha= ring via email, you might not have email set up for your browser.
